          </h3>

           Order online. All your favourite products from the low price online supermarket for grocery home delivery in Delhi, Gurgaon, Bengaluru, Mumbai and other cities in India. Lowest prices guaranteed on Patanjali, Aashirvaad, Pampers, Maggi, Saffola, Huggies, Fortune, Nestle, Amul, MamyPoko Pants, Surf Excel, Ariel, Vim, Haldiram's and others.

          <h3 class="footer-content__header" data-reactid="1332">
           One stop shop for all your daily needs
          </h3>
          <p class="footer-content__p" data-reactid="1333">
           Grofers is a low-price online supermarket that allows you to order products across categories like grocery, fruits &amp; vegetables, beauty &amp; wellness, household care, baby care, pet care and meats &amp; seafood and gets them delivered to your doorstep.
          </p>
          <h3 class="footer-content__header" data-reactid="1334">
           For best of prices, deals and offers; order online in cities
          </h3>
          <p class="footer-content__p" data-reactid="1335">
           The delivery service is operational in 25 cities: Agra, Ahmedabad, Bengaluru, Bhopal, Bhubaneswar, Chandigarh, Chennai, Delhi, Gurgaon, Hyderabad, Indore, Jaipur, Kanpur, Kochi, Kolkata, Lucknow, Ludhiana, Nagpur, Noida, Madurai, Mumbai, Pune, Ranchi, Surat and Vadodara.
